     <TITLE></TITLE>

<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0; color: #161616">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="text-align: right; font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0; color: #161616">Exhibit 99.1</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0; color: #161616">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0; color: #161616"><B>IBM Provides Update
to Management System and Reporting Segments</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #161616"><I>February 26, 2024</I></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>&nbsp;</I></P>

<P STYLE="text-indent: 0; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; color: #161616">As we enter 2024, we continue to advance
our hybrid cloud and AI strategy, with the completion of the Weather Company divestiture and updates to our management system. We are
making changes to our reportable segments, to reflect the way the company manages operations and allocates resources. These actions better
align our portfolio to our core strategy and to the underlying business models. These changes also provide more relevant information to
investors. The following updates do not impact IBM&rsquo;s consolidated results.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; color: #161616"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: normal">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD STYLE="padding-right: 24.45pt">The Weather Company divested assets moving from Software segment to Other &ndash; divested businesses</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 6.4pt 0pt 42pt; color: #161616">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; color: #161616">In August 2023 we announced the divestiture
of The Weather Company assets, and the transaction closed on January 31, 2024. In the first quarter of 2024, we realigned our management
structure to have these assets managed outside the Software segment, within Other &ndash; divested businesses (Other). The movement of
historical financials to Other is consistent with the treatment of other divested software and services content, and results in a Software
segment more closely aligned to its go-forward business.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; color: #161616"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: normal">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD>Security Services moving from Software to Consulting</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 11.55pt 0pt 42pt; color: #161616">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; color: #161616">To better capture the growing security
services market opportunity through our consulting engagements, management responsibility for Security Services has moved to Consulting.
Security Services will have greater access to Consulting clients globally and will be able to capitalize on the scale of Consulting&rsquo;s
operating model and discipline. As a result, Security Services, previously reported within the Software segment will move to the Consulting
segment.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; color: #161616"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Symbol; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: normal">&middot;</FONT></TD><TD>Improved transparency of segment profitability</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; color: #161616">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; color: #161616">IBM&rsquo;s reportable segments have
historically included stock-based compensation and net interest expense allocations. As those decisions are made at the corporate level,
these expenses have been removed from the business unit management system and will no longer be included in the reportable segments. This
provides improved transparency of segment profitability and better comparability to industry peers.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt; color: #161616">IBM&rsquo;s
reported results will reflect these changes beginning in the first quarter of 2024. We expect to</FONT> provide recast <FONT STYLE="color: #161616">segment
financials for 2022 and 2023 by the end of March to allow investors to update their models ahead of our first quarter earnings report.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-indent: 0; margin: 0pt 0; color: #161616">The 2024 expectations provided in our
January earnings call incorporated the divestiture of The Weather Company assets in the first quarter. Additionally, the commentary on
segment expectations applies to the recast segments.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-indent: 0; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="font-size: 10pt; border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%">
  <TR STYLE="font-size: 10pt; vertical-align: bottom">
    <TD STYLE="padding: 1pt 2pt; border-bottom: Black 2pt solid; font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; vertical-align: top; width: 49%; text-align: left">Reportable Segment Change</TD><TD STYLE="padding: 1pt 2pt; border-bottom: Black 2pt solid; font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; width: 2%">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 1pt 2pt; border-bottom: Black 2pt solid; font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; width: 49%; text-align: left">Resulting Segment Implications<BR>
 &nbsp;</TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="font-size: 10pt; vertical-align: bottom">
    <TD STYLE="padding: 1pt 2pt; border-bottom: Black 2pt solid; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; vertical-align: middle; text-align: left">The Weather Company asset divestiture</TD><TD STYLE="padding: 1pt 2pt; border-bottom: Black 2pt solid; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 1pt 2pt; border-bottom: Black 2pt solid; font-size: 10pt; text-align: left">- Software Segment<BR>
<BR>
+ Other &ndash; divested businesses</TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="font-size: 10pt; vertical-align: bottom">
    <TD STYLE="padding: 1pt 2pt; border-bottom: Black 2pt solid; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; vertical-align: middle; text-align: left">Security Services realignment</TD><TD STYLE="padding: 1pt 2pt; border-bottom: Black 2pt solid; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 1pt 2pt; border-bottom: Black 2pt solid; font-size: 10pt; text-align: left">- Software Segment<BR>
<BR>
+ Consulting Segment</TD></TR>
  <TR STYLE="font-size: 10pt; vertical-align: bottom">
    <TD STYLE="padding: 1pt 2pt; border-bottom: Black 2pt solid; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; vertical-align: middle; text-align: left">Removal of stock-based compensation and net interest expense allocations from segment profitability</TD><TD STYLE="padding: 1pt 2pt; border-bottom: Black 2pt solid; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</TD>
    <TD STYLE="padding: 1pt 2pt; border-bottom: Black 2pt solid; font-size: 10pt; text-align: left">- Software Segment, Consulting Segment, Infrastructure Segment, Financing Segment*<BR>
<BR>
+ Other</TD></TR>
  </TABLE>


<P STYLE="font: 14pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>*Presentation of interest for the Financing segment will
not change</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 6pt"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 2; Options: Last -->
